What is an </Value><I><Value>un-translation</Value></I><Value>? Bibles are translated into each of our languages from the original Hebrew, Aramaic, and Koine Greek. Occasionally, the best word translation cannot be found and these words are transliterated letter by letter. Four well known transliterations are </Value><I><Value>Christ</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>baptism</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>angel</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>apostle</Value></I><Value>. The meaning is then preserved more accurately through context and a dictionary. The Aionian Bible un-translates and instead transliterates ten additional Aionian Glossary words to help us better understand God’s love for individuals and all mankind, and the nature of afterlife destinies.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The first three words are </Value><I><Value>aiōn</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value>, typically translated as </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> and also </Value><I><Value>world</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value>. The Aionian Bible is named after an alternative spelling of </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value>. Consider that researchers question if </Value><I><Value>aiōn</Value></I><Value> and </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> actually mean </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value>. Translating </Value><I><Value>aiōn</Value></I><Value> as </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> in Matthew 28:20 makes no sense, as all agree. The Greek word for </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> is </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value>, used in Romans 1:20 about God and in Jude 6 about demon imprisonment. Yet what about </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> in John 3:16? Certainly we do not question whether salvation is eternal! However, </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> means something much more wonderful than infinite time! Ancient Greeks used </Value><I><Value>aiōn</Value></I><Value> to mean </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>age</Value></I><Value>. They also used the adjective </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> to mean </Value><I><Value>entirety</Value></I><Value>, such as </Value><I><Value>complete</Value></I><Value> or even </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value>, but never infinite time. Read Dr. Heleen Keizer and Ramelli and Konstan for proofs. So </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> is the perfect description of God's Word which has </Value><I><Value>everything</Value></I><Value> we need for life and godliness! And the </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> life promised in John 3:16 is not simply a ticket to eternal life in the future, but the invitation through faith to the </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value> life beginning now!</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The next seven words are </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Hadēs</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Tartaroō</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>Limnē Pyr</Value></I><Value>. These words are often translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>, the place of eternal punishment. However, </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> is ill-defined when compared with the Hebrew and Greek. For example, </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value> is the abode of deceased believers and unbelievers and should never be translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>. </Value><I><Value>Hadēs</Value></I><Value> is a temporary place of punishment, Revelation 20:13-14. </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value> is the Valley of Hinnom, Jerusalem's refuse dump, a temporal judgment for sin. </Value><I><Value>Tartaroō</Value></I><Value> is a prison for demons, mentioned once in 2 Peter 2:4. </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value> is a temporary prison for the Beast and Satan. Translators are also inconsistent because </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> is used by the King James Version 54 times, the New International Version 14 times, and the World English Bible zero times. Finally, </Value><I><Value>Limnē Pyr</Value></I><Value> is the Lake of Fire, yet Matthew 25:41 explains that these fires are prepared for the Devil and his angels. So there is reason to review our conclusions about the destinies of redeemed mankind and fallen angels.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>This </Value><I><Value>un-translation</Value></I><Value> helps us to see these ten underlying words in context. The original translation is unaltered and a note is added to 63 Old Testament and 200 New Testament verses. To help parallel study and Strong's Concordance use, apocryphal text is removed and most variant verse numbering is mapped to the English standard. The original translation is unaltered and notes are added to help your study. The notes show the location of ten special Greek and Hebrew Aionian Glossary words to help us better understand God’s love for individuals and for all mankind, and the nature of afterlife destinies.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Who has the authority to interpret the Bible and examine the underlying Hebrew and Greek words? That is a good question! We read in 1 John 2:27, </Value><I><Value>“As for you, the anointing which you received from him remains in you, and you do not need for anyone to teach you. But as his anointing teaches you concerning all things, and is true, and is no lie, and even as it taught you, you remain in him.”</Value></I><Value> Every Christian is qualified to interpret the Bible! Now that does not mean we will all agree. Each of us is still growing in our understanding of the truth. However, it does mean that there is no infallible human or tradition to answer all our questions. Instead the Holy Spirit helps each of us to know the truth and grow closer to God and each other.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Bible is a library with 66 books in the Protestant Canon. The best way to learn God’s word is to read entire books. Read the book of Genesis. Read the book of John. Read the entire Bible library. Topical studies and cross-referencing can be good. However, the safest way to understand context and meaning is to read whole Bible books. Chapter and verse numbers were added for convenience in the 16th century, but unfortunately they can cause the Bible to seem like an encyclopedia. The Aionian Bible is formatted with simple verse numbering, minimal notes, and no cross-referencing in order to encourage the reading of Bible books.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Bible reading must also begin with prayer. Any Christian is qualified to interpret the Bible with God’s help. However, this freedom is also a responsibility because without the Holy Spirit we cannot interpret accurately. We read in 1 Corinthians 2:13-14, </Value><I><Value>“And we speak of these things, not with words taught by human wisdom, but with those taught by the Spirit, comparing spiritual things with spiritual things. Now the natural person does not receive the things of the Spirit of God, for they are foolishness to him, and he cannot understand them, because they are spiritually discerned.”</Value></I><Value> So we cannot understand in our natural self, but we can with God’s help through prayer.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Holy Spirit is the best writer and he uses literary devices such as introductions, conclusions, paragraphs, and metaphors. He also writes various genres including historical narrative, prose, and poetry. So Bible study must spiritually discern and understand literature. Pray, read, observe, interpret, and apply. Finally, </Value><I><Value>“Do your best to present yourself approved by God, a worker who does not need to be ashamed, properly handling the word of truth.”</Value></I><Value> 2 Timothy 2:15. </Value><I><Value>“God has granted to us his precious and exceedingly great promises; that through these you may become partakers of the divine nature, having escaped from the corruption that is in the world by lust. Yes, and for this very cause adding on your part all diligence, in your faith supply moral excellence; and in moral excellence, knowledge; and in knowledge, self-control; and in self-control patience; and in patience godliness; and in godliness brotherly affection; and in brotherly affection, love. For if these things are yours and abound, they make you to be not idle nor unfruitful to the knowledge of our Lord Jesus Christ,”</Value></I><Value> 2 Peter 1:4-8.</Value></Paragraph>	<Paragraph textformat='center' fontfamily='FF-Head'><Value>Glossary</Value><Br /><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Pref'><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Glossar</Value></U><Value>y</Value></Fontface></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Aionian Bible un-translates and instead transliterates ten special words to help us better understand the extent of God’s love for individuals and all mankind, and the nature of afterlife destinies. /><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Pref'><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Bibles/English---Aionian-Bible/Noted</Value></U></Fontface></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Glossary references are below. Strong's Hebrew and Greek number notes are added to 63 Old Testament and 200 New Testament verses.  Questioned verse translations do not contain Aionian Glossary words and may wrongly imply </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>. * The note placement is skipped or adjusted for verses with non-standard numbering.</Value></Paragraph>	<Paragraph textformat='center' fontfamily='FF-Head'><Value>Prepared for the Devil and his Angels</Value><Br /><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Pref'><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Lake-of-Fire</Value></U></Fontface></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Aionian Bible shows the location of ten special Greek and Hebrew Aionian Glossary words to help us better understand God’s love for individuals and for all mankind, and the nature of after-life destinies. The underlying Hebrew and Greek words typically translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> show us that there are not just two after-life destinies, Heaven or Hell.  Instead, there are a number of different locations, each with different purposes, different durations, and different inhabitants. Locations include 1) Old Testament </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value> and New Testament </Value><I><Value>Hadēs</Value></I><Value>, 2) </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value>, 3) </Value><I><Value>Tartaroō</Value></I><Value>, 4) </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value>, 5) </Value><I><Value>Limnē Pyr</Value></I><Value>, 6) </Value><I><Value>Paradise</Value></I><Value>, 7) </Value><I><Value>The New Heaven</Value></I><Value>, and 8) </Value><I><Value>The New Earth</Value></I><Value>. So there is reason to review our conclusions about the destinies of redeemed mankind and fallen angels.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The key observation is that fallen angels will be present at the final judgment, 2 Peter 2:4 and Jude 6. Traditionally, we understand the separation of the Sheep and the Goats at the final judgment to mean separating believing from unbelieving mankind, Matthew 25:31-46 and Revelation 20:11-15. However, the presence of fallen angels at the final judgment alternatively suggests that Jesus is separating redeemed mankind from the fallen angels. We do know that Jesus is the helper of mankind and not the helper of the Devil, Hebrews 2.  We also know that Jesus has atoned for the sins of all mankind, both believer and unbeliever alike, 1 John 2:1-2. Certainly, unbelievers are punished in Hades as the story of Lazarus makes plain, Luke 16:19-31. Yet less commonly known, the punishment of this selfish man and all unbelievers is before the final judgment, is temporal, and is punctuated when Hades is evacuated, Revelation 20:13.  So is there hope beyond Hades for unbelieving mankind? Jesus promised, </Value><I><Value>“the gates of Hades will not prevail,”</Value></I><Value> Matthew 16:18. Paul asks, </Value><I><Value>“Hades where is your victory?”</Value></I><Value> 1 Corinthians 15:55. John wrote, </Value><I><Value>“Hades gives up,”</Value></I><Value> Revelation 20:13.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Jesus comforts us saying, </Value><I><Value>“Do not be afraid,”</Value></I><Value> because he holds the keys to </Value><I><Value>unlock</Value></I><Value> death and Hades, Revelation 1:18.  Yet too often our </Value><I><Value>Good News</Value></I><Value> sounds like a warning to </Value><I><Value>“be afraid”</Value></I><Value> because Jesus holds the keys to  </Value><I><Value>lock</Value></I><Value> Hades!  Wow, we have it backwards!  Hades will be evacuated!  And to guarrantee hope, once emptied, Hades is thrown into the Lake of Fire, never needed again, Revelation 20:14.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Finally, we read that anyone whose name is not written in the Book of Life is thrown into the Lake of Fire, the second death, with no exit ever mentioned or promised, Revelation 21:1-8.  So are those evacuated from Hades then, </Value><I><Value>“out of the frying pan, into the fire?”</Value></I><Value> Certainly, the Lake of Fire is the destiny of the Goats.  But, do not be afraid. Instead, read the Bible's explicit mention of the purpose of the Lake of Fire and the identity of the Goats, </Value><I><Value>“Then he will say also to those on the left hand, ‘Depart from me, you cursed, into the consummate fire which is prepared for the devil and his angels,’”</Value></I><Value> Matthew 25:41. Good news for all mankind!</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Faith is not a pen to write your own name in the Book of Life. Instead, faith is the glasses to see that the love of Christ for all mankind has already written our names in Heaven. Jesus said, </Value><I><Value>“You did not choose me, but I chose you,” John 15:16</Value></I><Value>. Though unbelievers will suffer regrettable punishment in Hades, redeemed mankind will never enter the Lake of Fire, prepared for the devil and his angels. And as God promised, all mankind will worship Christ together forever, Philippians 2:9-11.</Value></Paragraph>	GOOD		Preface				APPENDIX	Reader's Guide	Glossary	Maps	Illustrations																											END

المحتويات	الملحق	دليل القارئ	المعجم	خرائط	الرسوم التوضيحية	حياة	ترجمة الكتاب المقدس الأول في العالم عكس	100% مجانا لنسخ وطباعة	المعروف أيضا باسم	الكتاب المقدس الأرجواني	FOREIGN		6	لِأَنَّهُ هَكَذَا أَحَبَّ ٱللهُ ٱلْعَالَمَ حَتَّى بَذَلَ ٱبْنَهُ ٱلْوَحِيدَ، لِكَيْ لَا يَهْلِكَ كُلُّ مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِهِ، بَلْ تَكُونُ لَهُ ٱلْحَيَاةُ ٱلْأَبَدِيَّةُ.	يوحنَّا ٣:١٦	فَطَرَدَ ٱلْإِنْسَانَ، وَأَقَامَ شَرْقِيَّ جَنَّةِ عَدْنٍ ٱلْكَرُوبِيمَ، وَلَهِيبَ سَيْفٍ مُتَقَلِّبٍ لِحِرَاسَةِ طَرِيقِ شَجَرَةِ ٱلْحَيَاةِ.	اَلتَّكْوِينُ ٣:٢٤	فَقَالَ يَسُوعُ: «يَا أَبَتَاهُ، ٱغْفِرْ لَهُمْ، لِأَنَّهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ مَاذَا يَفْعَلُونَ».  وَإِذِ ٱقْتَسَمُوا ثِيَابَهُ ٱقْتَرَعُوا عَلَيْهَا.	لُوقا ٢٣:٣٤	وَأَنَا يُوحَنَّا رَأَيْتُ ٱلْمَدِينَةَ ٱلْمُقَدَّسَةَ أُورُشَلِيمَ ٱلْجَدِيدَةَ نَازِلَةً مِنَ ٱلسَّمَاءِ مِنْ عِنْدِ ٱللهِ مُهَيَّأَةً كَعَرُوسٍ مُزَيَّنَةٍ لِرَجُلِهَا. وَسَمِعْتُ صَوْتًا عَظِيمًا مِنَ ٱلسَّمَاءِ قَائِلًا: «هُوَذَا مَسْكَنُ ٱللهِ مَعَ ٱلنَّاسِ، وَهُوَ سَيَسْكُنُ مَعَهُمْ، وَهُمْ يَكُونُونَ لَهُ شَعْبًا، وَٱللهُ نَفْسُهُ يَكُونُ مَعَهُمْ إِلَهًا لَهُمْ.	رُؤيا ٢١:٢-٣	بِٱلْإِيمَانِ إِبْرَاهِيمُ لَمَّا دُعِيَ أَطَاعَ أَنْ يَخْرُجَ إِلَى ٱلْمَكَانِ ٱلَّذِي كَانَ عَتِيدًا أَنْ يَأْخُذَهُ مِيرَاثًا، فَخَرَجَ وَهُوَ لَا يَعْلَمُ إِلَى أَيْنَ يَأْتِي.	عِبرانِيّين ١١:٨	وَكَانَ لَمَّا أَطْلَقَ فِرْعَوْنُ ٱلشَّعْبَ أَنَّ ٱللهَ لَمْ يَهْدِهِمْ فِي طَرِيقِ أَرْضِ ٱلْفِلِسْطِينِيِّينَ مَعَ أَنَّهَا قَرِيبَةٌ، لِأَنَّ ٱللهَ قَالَ: «لِئَلَّا يَنْدَمَ ٱلشَّعْبُ إِذَا رَأَوْا حَرْبًا وَيَرْجِعُوا إِلَى مِصْرَ».	اَلْخُرُوجُ ١٣:١٧	لِأَنَّ ٱبْنَ ٱلْإِنْسَانِ أَيْضًا لَمْ يَأْتِ لِيُخْدَمَ بَلْ لِيَخْدِمَ وَلِيَبْذِلَ نَفْسَهُ فِدْيَةً عَنْ كَثِيرِينَ».	مَرْقُس ١٠:٤٥	بُولُسُ، عَبْدٌ لِيَسُوعَ ٱلْمَسِيحِ، ٱلْمَدْعُوُّ رَسُولًا، ٱلْمُفْرَزُ لِإِنْجِيلِ ٱللهِ،	رُوما ١:١	فَٱذْهَبُوا وَتَلْمِذُوا جَمِيعَ ٱلْأُمَمِ وَعَمِّدُوهُمْ بِٱسْمِ ٱلْآبِ وَٱلِٱبْنِ وَٱلرُّوحِ ٱلْقُدُسِ.	مَتَّى ٢٨:١٩	END

أَحَبَّ اللهُ الْعَالَمَ حَتَّى بَذَلَ ابْنَهُ الْوَحِيدَ، لِكَيْ لاَ يَهْلِكَ كُلُّ مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِهِ، بَلْ تَكُونُ لَهُ الْحَيَاةُ الأَبَدِيَّةُ.	يوحنَّا ٣:١٦	وَهَكَذَا طَرَدَ اللهُ الإِنْسَانَ مِنْ جَنَّةِ عَدْنٍ، وَأَقَامَ مَلائِكَةَ الْكَرُوبِيمِ وَسَيْفاً نَارِيّاً مُتَقَلِّباً شَرْقِيَّ الْجَنَّةِ لِحِرَاسَةِ الطَّرِيقِ الْمُفْضِيَةِ إِلَى «شَجَرَةِ الْحَيَاةِ».	تكوين ٣:٢٤	وَقَالَ يَسُوعُ: «يَاأَبِي، اغْفِرْ لَهُمْ، لأَنَّهُمْ لاَ يَدْرُونَ مَا يَفْعَلُونَ!» وَاقْتَسَمُوا ثِيَابَهُ مُقْتَرِعِينَ عَلَيْهَا.	لُوقا ٢٣:٣٤	وَأَنَا رَأَيْتُ الْمَدِينَةَ الْمُقَدَّسَةَ، أُورُشَلِيمَ الْجَدِيدَةَ، نَازِلَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللهِ، مُجَهَّزَةً كَأَنَّهَا عَرُوسٌ مُزَيَّنَةٌ لِعَرِيسِهَا. وَسَمِعْتُ صَوْتاً هَاتِفاً مِنَ الْعَرْشِ: «الآنَ صَارَ مَسْكِنُ اللهِ مَعَ النَّاسِ، هُوَ يَسْكُنُ بَيْنَهُمْ، وَهُمْ يَصِيرُونَ شَعْباً لَهُ.  اللهُ نَفْسُهُ يَكُونُ مَعَهُمْ إِلهاً لَهُمْ!	رُؤيا ٢١:٢-٣	وَبِالإِيمَانِ، لَبَّى إِبْرَاهِيمُ دَعْوَةَ اللهِ، فَتَرَكَ وَطَنَهُ وَانْطَلَقَ إِلَى أَرْضٍ أُخْرَى وَعَدَهُ اللهُ بِأَنْ يُوَرِّثَهُ إِيَّاهَا.  وَلَمَّا خَرَجَ مِنْ بَيْتِهِ، لَمْ يَكُنْ يَعْرِفُ أَيْنَ يَتَوَجَّهُ.	عِبرانِيّين ١١:٨	وَعِنْدَمَا أَطْلَقَ فِرْعَوْنُ الشَّعْبَ لَمْ يَقُدْهُمُ اللهُ فِي طَرِيقِ بِلاَدِ الْفِلِسْطِينِيِّينَ عَلَى الرَّغْمِ مِنْ قِصَرِهَا.  لأَنَّ اللهَ قَالَ لِئَلاَّ يَنْدَمَ الشَّعْبُ إِذَا تَعَرَّضَ لِحَرْبٍ وَيَرْجِعَ إِلَى مِصْرَ.	خرُوج ١٣:١٧	فَحَتَّى ابْنُ الإِنْسَانِ قَدْ جَاءَ لاَ لِيُخْدَمَ، بَلْ لِيَخْدِمَ وَيَبْذِلَ نَفْسَهُ فِدْيَةً عَنْ كَثِيرِينَ».	مَرْقُس ١٠:٤٥	مِنْ بُولُسَ عَبْدِ يَسُوعَ المَسِيحِ، الرَّسُولِ الْمَدْعُوِّ وَالْمُفْرَزِ لإِنْجِيلِ اللهِ،	رُوما ١:١	فَاذْهَبُوا إِذَنْ، وَتَلْمِذُوا جَمِيعَ الأُمَمِ، وَعَمِّدُوهُمْ بِاسْمِ الآبِ وَالاِبْنِ وَالرُّوحِ الْقُدُسِ؛	مَتَّى ٢٨:١٩	END

Աստուած ի՛նք պիտի ըլլայ անոնց հետ՝ իբր անոնց Աստուածը:	ՅԱՅՏՆՈՒԹԻՒՆ ՅՈՎՀԱՆՆՈՒ 21:2-3	Հաւատքո՛վ Աբրահամ հնազանդեցաւ, երբ կանչուեցաւ մեկնելու տեղ մը՝ որ պիտի ստանար իբր ժառանգութիւն,</Value><Br /><Value>ու մեկնեցաւ՝ առանց գիտնալու թէ ո՛ւր կ՚երթար:	ԵԲՐԱՅԵՑԻՍ 11:8	Երբ փարաւոնն արձակեց ժողովրդին, Աստուած նրանց կարճ ճանապարհով՝ Փղշտացիների երկրով չառաջնորդեց,</Value><Br /><Value>որովհետեւ Աստուած մտածեց, թէ ժողովուրդը պատերազմի բռնուելով՝ գուցէ վախենայ ու Եգիպտոս վերադառնայ:	ԵԼՔ 13:17	Քանի որ մարդու Որդին եկաւ ո՛չ թէ սպասարկութիւն ընդունելու, հապա՝ սպասարկելու եւ իր անձը իբր փրկանք տալու շատերու համար:</Value><Br /><Value>	ՄԱՐԿՈՍ 10:45	Պօղոս, ծառայ Յիսուս Քրիստոսի, կանչուած՝ առաքեալ ըլլալու, նշանակուած՝ քարոզելու Աստուծոյ աւետարանը,	ՀՌՈՎՄԱՅԵՑԻՍ 1:1	Ուրեմն գացէ՛ք, աշակերտեցէ՛ք բոլոր ազգերը, մկրտեցէ՛ք զանոնք Հօր, Որդիին եւ Սուրբ Հոգիին անունով:</Value><Br /><Value>	ՄԱՏԹԷՈՍ 28:19	END

তাৰ পাছত জীৱন-বৃক্ষৰ ওচৰলৈ যোৱাৰ পথ ৰখিবলৈ, এদন বাৰীৰ পুবফালে কৰূবসকলক ৰাখিলে আৰু চাৰিওফালে ঘূৰি থকা এখন জলন্তময় তৰোৱালকো তাত থলে।	আদিপুস্তক ৩:২৪	তেতিয়া যীচুৱে ক’লে, “হে পিতৃ, এওঁলোকক ক্ষমা কৰা; কিয়নো এওঁলোকে কি কৰিছে, সেই বিষয়ে নাজানে।” পাছত তেওঁলোকে চিঠি খেলি তেওঁৰ বস্ত্ৰ ভগাই ললে।	লূক ২৩:৩৪	আৰু দৰাৰ কাৰণে বিভূষিতা কন্যা যেনে, তেনেকৈ যুগুত হোৱা, সেই পবিত্ৰ নগৰ নতুন যিৰূচালেমক, ঈশ্বৰৰ পৰা, অৰ্থাৎ স্বৰ্গৰ পৰা নমা দেখিলোঁ। পাছত মই সেই সিংহাসনৰ পৰা এই মহা আকাশ-বাণী শুনিলোঁ, “সৌৱা চোৱা!”  লোক সকলৰ সহিত ঈশ্বৰৰ নিবাস আৰু তেওঁলোকৰ সহিত তেওঁ নিবাস কৰিব৷ তেওঁলোক তেওঁৰ নিজ লোক হব, আৰু ঈশ্বৰ নিজে সঙ্গী হৈ তেওঁলোকৰ ঈশ্বৰ হ’ব৷	প্ৰকাশিত বাক্য ২১:২-৩	ঈশ্বৰত বিশ্বাস আছিল কাৰণে ঈশ্বৰে যেতিয়া অব্ৰাহামক আহ্বান কৰিলে, তেতিয়া তেওঁ বাধ্য হ’ল, আৰু তেওঁক যি দেশ দিম বুলি ঈশ্বৰে কৈছিল, সেই দেশ অধিকাৰ কৰিবৰ বাবে তেওঁ গৈছিল; আৰু ক’লৈ যাব লাগে, সেই বিষয়ে নাজানিও ওলাই গৈছিল।	ইব্ৰী ১১:৮	ফৰৌণে যেতিয়া লোকসকলক যাবলৈ এৰি দিলে, তেতিয়া পলেষ্টীয়াসকলৰ দেশেৰে বাট চমু আছিল যদিও, ঈশ্বৰে তেওঁলোকক সেই বাটেদি নিনিলে।</Value><Br /><Value>কিয়নো ঈশ্বৰে ক’লে, “হয়তো যুদ্ধৰ সন্মুখিন হ’লে লোকসকলে মন সলনি কৰি মিচৰলৈ উভটি যাব।”	যাত্রাপুস্তক ১৩:১৭	কিয়নো মানুহৰ পুত্ৰ সেৱা শুশ্ৰূষা পাবৰ বাবে নহয়, কিন্তু সেৱা শুশ্ৰূষা কৰিবলৈ আৰু অনেকৰ মুক্তিৰ মূল্যৰ অৰ্থে নিজৰ প্ৰাণ দিবলৈহে আহিল।	মাৰ্ক ১০:৪৫	মই পৌল, যীচু খ্ৰীষ্টৰ এজন দাস আৰু ঈশ্বৰৰ শুভবাৰ্তাৰ কাৰণে পৃথক হোৱা আমন্ত্ৰিত পাঁচনি;	ৰোমীয়া ১:১	এই হেতুকে, তোমালোক যোৱা; আৰু সকলো জাতিকে শিষ্য কৰি, পিতৃ, পুত্ৰ আৰু পবিত্ৰ আত্মাৰ নামেৰে তেওঁলোকক বাপ্তাইজ কৰা;	মথি ২৮:১৯	END

Holy-Bible---English---Aionian-Bible				TRUE	TRUE	978-0-35939-420-3	978-1-67811-695-8	978-1-67811-689-7	978-0-35937-112-9	b04daed1-f0b2-4f6f-bb14-4ba2af9e871f			Aionian Bible	Aionian Bible																		FF-Copy	FF-VerE	758				125.88%		0.0000			0.0000			<Paragraph textformat='center' fontfamily='FF-Head'><Value>Preface</Value><Br /><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Pref'><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Preface</Value></U></Fontface></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The </Value><I><Value>Holy Bible Aionian Edition ®</Value></I><Value> is the world’s first Bible </Value><I><Value>un-translation</Value></I><Value>! What is an </Value><I><Value>un-translation</Value></I><Value>? Bibles are translated into each of our languages from the original Hebrew, Aramaic, and Greek. Occasionally, the best word translation cannot be found and these words are transliterated letter by letter. Four well known transliterations are </Value><I><Value>Christ</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>baptism</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>angel</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>apostle</Value></I><Value>. The meaning is then preserved more accurately through context and a dictionary. The Aionian Bible un-translates and instead transliterates ten additional Aionian Glossary words to help us better understand God’s love for individuals and all mankind, and the nature of afterlife destinies.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Aionian Bible </Value><I><Value>un-translation</Value></I><Value> helps us to see these ten underlying words in context. Actually, the original translation is unaltered and a note is added to 63 Old Testament and 200 New Testament verses. Also the Aionian Bible is not one Bible, but an entire library of public domain and Creative Common Bible texts. In each of the Bible republications the original text is wholly unaltered, except for this particular translation which is specifically named the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation. The </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation is a new translation identical to the public domain </Value><I><Value>World English Bible</Value></I><Value> except for the retranslation of the verses containing Aionian Glossary words and a few additional verses are revised to correspond with the underlying Hebrew and Greek. This new translation includes the same inline notes as every Bible in the Aionian Bible library, but also retranslates the Aionian Glossary words to more accurately reflect the underlying Hebrew and Greek words.  Every verse retranslation in the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation is based on meticulous reference to the underlying language sources. The </Value><I><Value>World English Bible</Value></I><Value> was chosen as a base text simply because it is the most readable public domain English translation.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The first three Greek words reconsidered are </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value>, typically translated as </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> and also </Value><I><Value>world</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value>. In fact, the Aionian Bible is named after an alternative spelling of </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value>. Consider that researchers question if </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> and </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> actually mean </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value>. Translating </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> as </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> in Matthew 28:20 makes no sense, as all agree. The Greek word for </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> is </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value>, used in Romans 1:20 about God and in Jude 6 about demon imprisonment. Therefore, </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value> remains translated as </Value><I><Value>everlasting</Value></I><Value> in the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation. Yet what about </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> in John 3:16? Certainly we do not question whether salvation is eternal! However, </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> means something much more wonderful than infinite time! Ancient Greeks used </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> to mean </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>age</Value></I><Value>.  The similar spelling of </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> and </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value> is easily seen.  They also used the adjective </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> to mean </Value><I><Value>entirety</Value></I><Value>, such as </Value><I><Value>complete</Value></I><Value> or even </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value>, but never infinite time. Thus </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> is retranslated </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value> 65 times, </Value><I><Value>of the ages</Value></I><Value> two times, and </Value><I><Value>wholly</Value></I><Value> one time in the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation. </Value><I><Value>Aion</Value></I><Value> is retranslated as </Value><I><Value>age</Value></I><Value> 95 times and </Value><I><Value>lifetime</Value></I><Value> two times. Note that familiar Hebrews verses now say more accurately, and perhaps even more poetically, '</Value><I><Value>Jesus is a priest for the age.</Value></I><Value>'</Value></Paragraph> <Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The wonderful rediscovery is that the </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> life promised in John 3:16 is not simply a ticket to eternal life in the future, but the invitation through faith to the </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value> life beginning now!  </Value><I><Value>Aionios</Value></I><Value> is the perfect description of God's Word which has </Value><I><Value>everything</Value></I><Value> we need for life and godliness.</Value></Paragraph>	<Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The next seven words are </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Hades</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Tartaroo</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>Limne Pyr</Value></I><Value>. These words are often translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>, the place of eternal punishment. However, </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> is ill-defined when compared with the Hebrew and Greek. For example, </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value> is the abode of deceased believers and unbelievers and should never be translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>. </Value><I><Value>Hades</Value></I><Value> is a temporary place of punishment, Revelation 20:13-14. </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value> is the Valley of Hinnom, Jerusalem's refuse dump, a temporal judgment for sin. </Value><I><Value>Tartaroo</Value></I><Value> is a prison for demons, mentioned once in 2 Peter 2:4. </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value> is a temporary prison for the Beast and Satan. Translators are also inconsistent because </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> is used by the King James Version 54 times, the New International Version 14 times, and the </Value><I><Value>World English Bible</Value></I><Value> zero times.  Finally, </Value><I><Value>Limne Pyr</Value></I><Value> is the Lake of Fire, yet Matthew 25:41 explains that these fires are prepared for the Devil and his angels.  So there is reason to review our conclusions about the destinies of redeemed mankind and fallen angels.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Aionian Bible project invites you to reconsider traditional Christian understanding.  It may seem utterly ridiculous to suggest that the most well-known verse in the history of Christianity, John 3:16, was improperly translated.  And it may seem preposterous to propose that a destiny of Heaven or Hell is not the complete picture.  Yet is it ridiculous?  Is it preposterous?  Have we or our forefathers ever carried ignorance and errors along for decades and even centuries in the past?  We have.  Even so, the purpose of the Aionian Bible project is not to abandon tradition or Christian heritage.  We have much to learn from the belief and practice of godly men and women throughout all ages. Instead the purpose of this project is to invite us to compare our current conclusions with Scripture.  We should never be afraid to review our understanding.  Do consider Dr. Heleen Keizer's article </Value><I><Value>'ETERNITY REVISITED' A Study of the Greek Word aion</Value></I><Value> and other resources at </Value><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Aionios-and-Aidios</Value></U><Value>.  This article is a useful introduction to the first century usage and meaning of </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> and </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value>.  Further resources can be found countless places online and in print.  Then study the Scripture and ask the Lord for understanding.  Hopefully you find this invitation to reconsider fair, thought-provoking, and above all, honoring to God's Word.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Again, the original text for each translation in the Aionian Bible library is unaltered, except for this particular Bible named the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value>, which is itself a new translation based on the </Value><I><Value>World English Bible</Value></I><Value> as explained above. Holy-Bible---English---STEPBible-Amalgamant				TRUE	TRUE	UNKNOWN		UNKNOWN	UNKNOWN	621f287c-dc34-3d60-da90-2ecee6ceb0a5			STEPBible, Amalgamant	STEPBible, Amalgamant																		FF-Copy	FF-VerE	800		8.4000	10.6000	126.19%		2.2000			0.0000	This text is a Bible translator resource from the STEPBible Tyndale Amalgamated Hebrew and Greek. The Greek text is tagged 1) 'NA=TR' (default Nestle/Aland = Textus Receptus) 133,304 words from NA27/28+TR+others with same meaning, 2) 'NA~TR' 3,922 words from NA27/28 with different meanings in TR, 3) 'NA-TR' 761 words in NA27/28 not in TR, 4) 'KJV' 3,573 words in TR not in NA27/28, 5) 'KJV+' 3,573 words in TR+Older Bibles but not in NA27/28, 6) 'KJV++' 227 words in TR+Modern Bibles but not in NA27/28, and 7) 'NATR?' 245 words not found in NA27/28 or TR.  New Testament study is revolutionized by the discovery of earlier manuscripts in the North African sands and other discoveries.  The NA text is based mostly on these earlier manuscripts, but the TR text was compiled from later ones, before the earlier ones were found. Later scribes often removed ambiguities with changes like adding the name 'Jesus' instead of 'he', adding prepositions such as 'with' and 'to' instead of relying on Greek dative and genitive cases, and occasionally adding phrases to clarify the text. There are no instances of changed theology, confirmed by the huge failed effort to find even one. Less discussed are the words found in the earlier manuscripts, but not in the later.  Of these, there are 548 differences with no impact to meaning, and 277 scribal clarification differences. And these are only mildly significant changes like '72' for '70' disciples sent out in Luke 10:1,17, 'Spirit of Jesus' for 'Jesus' in Acts 16:7, 'as you now walk' in 1Th 4:1, 'according to God' in 1Pet 5:2, 'show mercy to others' in Jude 23, and 'and a third of the earth was burned' in Rev 8:7. The best explanation is that additions found only in earlier manuscripts and additions found only in later ones are simply two sets of additions by scribes to clarify the text with no theological agenda. So, if you want the very earliest text, use only the words that are in both NA and TR. If you want to include clarifications by North African believers like modern Bibles, then include words found only in NA. If you want to only include the clarifications by Byzantine scribes like the KJV, then include the words found only in TR, and use the TR variants.	<Paragraph textformat='leftpad' fontfamily='FF-Copy'><Value>This text is a Bible translator resource from the STEPBible Tyndale Amalgamated Hebrew and Greek. સીમાને સાચવવા તેમણે એદન વાડીની પૂર્વગમ અગ્નિરૂપી તરવાર સાથે કરુબોને ચોકીદાર તરીકે ગોઠવ્યા.	ઊત્પત્તિ ૩:૨૪	ઈસુએ કહ્યું, 'હે પિતા, તેઓને માફ કરો, કેમ કે તેઓ જે કરે છે તે તેઓ જાણતા નથી.'</Value><Br /><Value>ચિઠ્ઠીઓ નાખીને તેઓએ તેમના વસ્ત્ર અંદરોઅંદર વહેંચી લીધા.	લૂક ૨૩:૩૪	મેં પવિત્ર નગર, નવું યરુશાલેમ, ઈશ્વરની પાસેથી સ્વર્ગમાંથી ઊતરતું જોયું, અને જેમ કન્યા પોતાના વરને સારુ શણગારેલી હોય તેમ તે તૈયાર કરેલું હતું. રાજ્યાસનમાંથી મોટી વાણી એમ કહેતી મેં સાંભળી કે, 'જુઓ, ઈશ્વરનું રહેઠાણ માણસોની સાથે છે, અને ઈશ્વર તેઓની સાથે વસશે, અને તેઓ તેમના લોકો થશે, અને ઈશ્વર પોતે તેઓની સાથે રહીને તેઓના ઈશ્વર થશે.	પ્રકટીકરણ ૨૧:૨-૩	ઇબ્રાહિમ જે જગ્યા વારસામાં પામવાનો હતો, તેમાં જવાને તેડું પામીને આજ્ઞાધીન થયો, એટલે પોતે ક્યાં જાય છે, એ ન જાણ્યાં છતાં વિશ્વાસથી તે રવાના થયો.	હિબ્રૂઓને પત્ર ૧૧:૮	જ્યારે ફારુને લોકોને જવા દીઘા ત્યારે એમ બન્યું કે પલિસ્તીઓના દેશમાં થઈને જવાનો રસ્તો ટૂંકો હોવા છતાં પણ તે રસ્તે તેઓને લઈ ગયા નહિ.</Value><Br /><Value>કેમ કે યહોવાહે વિચાર્યું કે, “રખેને યુદ્ધ થાય અને લોકો પોતાનો વિચાર બદલી પાછા મિસર ચાલ્યા જાય.”	નિર્ગમન ૧૩:૧૭	કેમ કે માણસનો દીકરો સેવા કરાવવાને નહિ, પણ સેવા કરવાને, તથા ઘણાંનાં મુક્તિમૂલ્યને સારુ પોતાનો જીવ આપવાને આવ્યો છે.	માર્ક ૧૦:૪૫	પ્રેરિત થવા સારુ તેડાયેલો અને ઈશ્વરની સુવાર્તા માટે અલગ કરાયેલો ઈસુ ખ્રિસ્તનો સેવક પાઉલ.	રોમનોને પત્ર ૧:૧	એ માટે તમે જઈને સર્વ દેશનાઓને શિષ્ય કરો; પિતા તથા પુત્ર તથા પવિત્ર આત્માને નામે તેઓને બાપ્તિસ્મા આપતા જાઓ.	માથ્થી The underlying Hebrew and Greek words typically translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> show us that there are not just two after-life destinies, Heaven or Hell.  Instead, there are a number of different locations, each with different purposes, different durations, and different inhabitants. Locations include 1) Old Testament </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value> and New Testament </Value><I><Value>Hadēs</Value></I><Value>, 2) </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value>, 3) </Value><I><Value>Tartaroō</Value></I><Value>, 4) </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value>, 5) </Value><I><Value>Limnē Pyr</Value></I><Value>, 6) </Value><I><Value>Paradise</Value></I><Value>, 7) </Value><I><Value>The New Heaven</Value></I><Value>, and 8) </Value><I><Value>The New Earth</Value></I><Value>. So there is reason to review our conclusions about the destinies of redeemed mankind and fallen angels.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The most significant observation is that fallen angels will be present at the final judgment, 2 Peter 2:4 and Jude 6. Traditionally, we understand the separation of the Sheep and the Goats at the final judgment to mean separating believing from unbelieving mankind, Matthew 25:31-46 and Revelation 20:11-15. However, the presence of fallen angels at the final judgment alternatively suggests that Jesus is separating redeemed mankind from the fallen angels. We do know that Jesus is the helper of mankind and not the helper of the Devil, Hebrews 2.  We also know that Jesus has atoned for the sins of all mankind, both believer and unbeliever alike, 1 John 2:1-2. Certainly, unbelievers are punished for their selfishness as the story of Lazarus makes plain, Luke 16:19-31. Yet less commonly known, the punishment of this selfish man and all unbelievers is before the final judgment, is temporal, and is punctuated when Hades is evacuated, Revelation 20:13.  So is there hope beyond Hades for unbelieving mankind? Jesus promised, </Value><I><Value>“the gates of Hades will not prevail,”</Value></I><Value> Matthew 16:18. Paul asks, </Value><I><Value>“Hades where is your victory?”</Value></I><Value> 1 Corinthians 15:55. John wrote, </Value><I><Value>“Hades gives up,”</Value></I><Value> Revelation 20:13.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>We should find hope that Jesus tells us, </Value><I><Value>“Do not be afraid,”</Value></I><Value> because he holds the keys to </Value><I><Value>unlock</Value></I><Value> death and Hades, Revelation 1:18.  Yet too often our </Value><I><Value>Good News</Value></I><Value> sounds like a warning to </Value><I><Value>“be afraid”</Value></I><Value> because Jesus holds the keys to  </Value><I><Value>lock</Value></I><Value> Hades!  Wow, we have it backwards!  Hades will be evacuated!  And there is even greater hope because after the prison of Hades is evacuated, it is thrown into the Lake of Fire, never needed again, Revelation 20:14.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Finally, we read that anyone whose name is not written in the Book of Life is thrown into the Lake of Fire, the second death, with no exit ever mentioned or promised, Revelation 21:1-8.  So are those evacuated from Hades then, </Value><I><Value>“out of the frying pan, into the fire?”</Value></I><Value> Certainly, the Lake of Fire is the destiny of the Goats.  But, do not be afraid. Instead, read the Bible's explicit mention of the purpose of the Lake of Fire and the identity of the Goats, </Value><I><Value>“Then he will say also to those on the left hand, ‘Depart from me, </Value></I><Value>y</Value><I><Value>ou cursed, into the consummate fire which is prepared for the devil and his angels,’”</Value></I><Value> Matthew 25:41. Good news for all mankind!</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Faith is not a pen to write your own name in the Book of Life. Instead, faith is the glasses to see that the love of Christ for all mankind has already written our names in Heaven. Jesus said, </Value><I><Value>“You did not choose me, but I chose you,” John 15:16</Value></I><Value>. Though unbelievers will suffer regrettable punishment in Hades, redeemed mankind will never enter the Lake of Fire, prepared for the devil and his angels.</Value></Paragraph>	Translate	FOREIGN	הקדמה	הברית הישנה	עדות חדשה	תוכן העניינים	נספח	מדריך הקורא	מילון	מפות	איורים	החיים	התרגום ההפוך הראשון בעולם	הוא זמין להעתיק ולהדפיס	קראו לו גם	התנ'ך הסגול	FOREIGN		6	כי ככה אהב האלהים את העולם עד אשר נתן את בנו את יחידו למען לא יאבד כל המאמין בו כי אם יחיה חיי עולמים׃	ג'ון 3:16	ויגרש את האדם וישכן מקדם לגן עדן את הכרבים ואת להט החרב המתהפכת לשמר את דרך עץ החיים׃	בראשית 3:24	ויאמר ישוע אבי סלח להם כי לא ידעו מה הם עשים ויחלקו בגדיו להם ויפילו גורל׃	לוּקָס 23:34	וארא את העיר הקדושה ירושלים החדשה ירדת מאת האלהים מן השמים נכונה ככלה המקשטת לבעלה׃ ואשמע קול גדול מן השמים לאמר הנה משכן אלהים עם בני האדם ושכן בתוכם והמה יהיו לו לעם והוא האלהים יהיה אתם אלהיהם׃	חזוֹן יוֹחָנָן 21:2-3	באמונה שמע אברהם כאשר נקרא ללכת אל הארץ אשר יירשנה ויצא ולא ידע אנה יבוא׃	אֶל־הָעִבְרִים 11:8	ויהי בשלח פרעה את העם ולא נחם אלהים דרך ארץ פלשתים כי קרוב הוא כי אמר אלהים פן ינחם העם בראתם מלחמה ושבו מצרימה׃	שמות 13:17	כי בן האדם אף הוא לא בא למען ישרתוהו כי אם לשרת ולתת את נפשו כפר תחת רבים׃	מארק 10:45	פולוס עבד ישוע המשיח מקרא להיות שליח ונבדל לבשורת אלהים׃	אֶל־הָרוֹמִיִּים 1:1	לכו ועשו לתלמידים את כל הגוים וטבלתם אתם לשם האב והבן ורוח הקדש׃	מתיו 28:19	END

ထာ​ဝ​ရ​အ​သက်​ကို​ရ​စေ​ခြင်း​ငှာ မိ​မိ ၏​တစ်​ပါး​တည်း​သော​သား​တော်​ကို​စွန့်​တော် မူ​၏။	ရှင်ယောဟန် ၃:၁၆	ထို​နောက်​အ​သက်​ရှင်​စေ​သော​အ​ပင်​အ​နီး သို့​မည်​သူ​မျှ​မ​ချဉ်း​ကပ်​နိုင်​စေ​ရန် လည်​ပတ် လျက်​ရှိ​သော​ဋ္ဌား​မီး​စက်​လက်​နက်​နှင့်​တ​ကွ ခေ​ရု​ဗိမ် တို့​ကို​ဥယျာဉ်​အ​ရှေ့​ဘက်​တွင်​အ​စောင့်​ချ ထား​တော်​မူ​၏။	ကမ္ဘာ​ဦး ၃:၂၄	သ​ခင်​ယေ​ရှု​က ``အို အ​ဖ၊ ထို​သူ​တို့​၏​အ​ပြစ် ကို​ဖြေ​လွှတ်​တော်​မူ​ပါ။ သူ​တို့​သည်​မိ​မိ​တို့​ပြု နေ​သည့်​အ​မှု​ကို​မ​သိ​ကြ​ပါ'' ဟု​မြွက်​ဆို တော်​မူ​၏။ သူ​တို့​သည်​ကိုယ်​တော်​၏​အ​ဝတ်​တော်​များ​ကို မဲ​ချ​၍​ဝေ​ယူ​ကြ​၏။	လုကာ ၂၃:၃၄	ဘု​ရား​သ​ခင်​စံ​တော်​မူ​ရာ​ကောင်း​ကင်​ဘုံ​မှ သန့်​ရှင်း​မြင့်​မြတ်​သော​မြို့​ကြီး​ဖြစ်​သည့်​ယေ​ရု ရှ​လင်​မြို့​သစ်​သည် သ​တို့​သား​အ​တွက်​အ​ဝတ် တန်​ဆာ​ဆင်​ယင်​ထား​သည့်​သ​တို့​သ​မီး​ကဲ့​သို့ ပြင်​ဆင်​လျက်​သက်​ဆင်း​လာ​သည်​ကို​ငါ​မြင် ရ​၏။- ငါ​သည်​ပလ္လင်​တော်​မှ​ကျယ်​စွာ​သော​အ​သံ​ကို ကြား​ရ​၏။ ထို​အ​သံ​က``ယ​ခု​အ​ခါ​၌​ဘု​ရား သ​ခင်​သည်​လူ​သား​တို့​ထံ​တွင်​ကျိန်း​ဝပ်​တော် မူ​ပြီ။ ကိုယ်​တော်​သည်​သူ​တို့​နှင့်​အ​တူ​နေ​တော် မူ​မည်။ ထို​သူ​တို့​သည်​ကိုယ်​တော်​၏​လူ​စု​တော် ဖြစ်​ကြ​လိမ့်​မည်။ ဘု​ရား​သ​ခင်​ကိုယ်​တော်​တိုင် ပင်​လျှင်​သူ​တို့​နှင့်​အ​တူ​ရှိ​နေ​တော်​မူ​၍​သူ တို့​၏​ဘု​ရား​ဖြစ်​မည်။	ဗျာ​ဒိတ် ၂၁:၂-၃	အာ​ဗြ​ဟံ​သည်​ဘု​ရား​သ​ခင်​ခေါ်​တော်​မူ သော​အ​ခါ ကိုယ်​တော်​၏​စ​ကား​ကို​နား​ထောင်​၍ မိ​မိ​အား​က​တိ​ထား​တော်​မူ​သော​ပြည်​သို့ ယုံ​ကြည်​ခြင်း​အား​ဖြင့်​ထွက်​ခွာ​သွား​၏။ သူ သည်​အ​ဘယ်​အ​ရပ်​သို့​သွား​ရ​မည်​ကို မ​သိ​ဘဲ မိ​မိ​၏​ရပ်​ရွာ​ကို​စွန့်​ခဲ့​ပေ​သည်။	ဟေ​ဗြဲ ၁၁:၈	အီ​ဂျစ်​ဘု​ရင်​သည်​ဣသ​ရေ​လ​အ​မျိုး​သား တို့​အား​ထွက်​ခွင့်​ပြု​သော​အ​ခါ ထာ​ဝ​ရ ဘု​ရား​သည်​ဖိ​လိတ္တိ​မြို့​သို့​သွား​သော​ပင် လယ်​ကမ်း​ခြေ​ဖြတ်​လမ်း​ဖြင့် သူ​တို့​ကို​ပို့ ဆောင်​တော်​မ​မူ။ သူ​တို့​သည်​စစ်​ပွဲ​တိုက်​ရ​မည် ကို​သိ​မြင်​လျှင်​စိတ်​ပြောင်း​၍ အီ​ဂျစ်​ပြည် သို့​ပြန်​သွား​ကြ​မည်​ဖြစ်​ကြောင်း​ဘု​ရား​သ​ခင်​သိ​တော်​မူ​၏။	ထွက်​မြောက် ၁၃:၁၇	လူ​သား​ပင်​လျှင်​သူ​တစ်​ပါး​အား​စေ​စား​ရန် ကြွ​လာ​သည်​မ​ဟုတ်။ သူ​တစ်​ပါး​၏ အ​စေ​ကို ခံ​ရန်​လည်း​ကောင်း၊ မိ​မိ​အ​သက်​ကို​စွန့်​၍​လူ အ​မြောက်​အ​မြား​အား​ရွေး​နုတ်​ရန်​လည်း ကောင်း​ကြွ​လာ​သ​တည်း​ဟု​မိန့်​တော်​မူ​၏။	ရှင်မာကု ၁၀:၄၅	သ​တင်း​ကောင်း​ကို​ကြေ​ညာ​ရန်​တ​မန်​တော် အ​ဖြစ်​ဖြင့် ဘု​ရား​သ​ခင်​ရွေး​ချယ်​ခန့်​ထား​သူ၊ ခ​ရစ်​တော်​ယေ​ရှု​၏​အ​စေ​ခံ​ငါ​ပေါ​လု​သည် စာ​ရေး​လိုက်​ပါ​သည်။	ရော​မ ၁:၁	သို့​ဖြစ်​၍​သင်​တို့​သည်​သွား​၍​လူ​မျိုး​တ​ကာ​တို့ ପୁଣି, ଅମୃତ ବୃକ୍ଷର ପଥ ରକ୍ଷା କରିବା ନିମିତ୍ତ ଏଦନ ଉଦ୍ୟାନର ପୂର୍ବଦିଗରେ କିରୂବଗଣ ଓ ଚତୁର୍ଦ୍ଦିଗରେ ଘୂର୍ଣ୍ଣାୟମାନ ତେଜୋମୟ ଖଡ୍ଗ ସ୍ଥାପନ କଲେ।	ମୋଶାଙ୍କ ଲିଖିତ ପ୍ରଥମ ପୁସ୍ତକ ୩:୨୪	ସେତେବେଳେ ଯୀଶୁ କହିଲେ, ପିତଃ, ଏମାନଙ୍କୁ କ୍ଷମା କର, କାରଣ ଏମାନେ କ'ଣ କରୁଅଛନ୍ତି, ତାହା ଜାଣନ୍ତି ନାହିଁ ।</Value><Br /><Value>ଆଉ ସେମାନେ ତାହାଙ୍କ ବସ୍ତ୍ରସବୁ ଭାଗ କରିବା ନିମନ୍ତେ ଗୁଲିବାଣ୍ଟ କଲେ ।	ଲୂକ ୨୩:୩୪	ପୁଣି, ମୁଁ ପବିତ୍ର ନଗରୀ, ଅର୍ଥାତ୍ ନୂତନ ଯିରୁଶାଲମକୁ ବର ନିମନ୍ତେ ସଜ୍ଜିତା କନ୍ୟାର ସଦୃଶ ପ୍ରସ୍ତୁତା ହୋଇ ସ୍ୱର୍ଗରୁ ଈଶ୍ୱରଙ୍କ ନିକଟରୁ ଅବତରଣ କରିବାର ଦେଖିଲି । ଆଉ ମୁଁ ସିଂହାସନ ମଧ୍ୟରୁ ଗୋଟିଏ ମହା ଶଦ୍ଦ ଏହା କହିବାର ଶୁଣିଲି, ଦେଖ, ମନୁଷ୍ୟମାନଙ୍କ ମଧ୍ୟରେ ଈଶ୍ୱରଙ୍କ</Value><Br /><Value>ବାସସ୍ଥାନ ଅଛି, ସେ ସେମାନଙ୍କ ସହିତ ବାସ କରିବେ, ଆଉ ସେମାନେ ତାହାଙ୍କ ଲୋକ ହେବେ,	ପ୍ରକାଶିତ ୨୧:୨-୩	ବିଶ୍ୱାସ ଦ୍ୱାରା ଅବ୍ରହାମ ଆହ୍ୱାନ ପ୍ରାପ୍ତ ହୁଅନ୍ତେ, ଯେଉଁ ଦେଶ ସେ ଅଧିକାରସ୍ୱରୂପେ ପାଇବାକୁ ଯାଉଥିଲେ, ଆଜ୍ଞାବହ ହୋଇ ସେଠାକୁ ବାହାରିଗଲେ, ପୁଣି, ସେ କେଉଁଠାକୁ ଯାଉଅଛନ୍ତି, ତାହା ନ ଜାଣି ସୁଦ୍ଧା ବାହାରିଗଲେ ।	ଏବ୍ରୀ ୧୧:୮	ଏଥିଉତ୍ତାରେ ଫାରୋ ଲୋକମାନଙ୍କୁ ଯିବାକୁ ଦିଅନ୍ତେ, ପଲେଷ୍ଟୀୟ ଲୋକମାନଙ୍କର ଦେଶକୁ ଯିବାର ପଥ ନିକଟ ହେଲେ ହେଁ ପରମେଶ୍ୱର ସେହି ପଥରେ ସେମାନଙ୍କୁ ଗମନ କରାଇଲେ ନାହିଁ;</Value><Br /><Value>ଯେହେତୁ ପରମେଶ୍ୱର କହିଲେ, “ଯେବେ ଲୋକମାନେ ଯୁଦ୍ଧ ଦେଖନ୍ତି ସେମାନେ ଆପଣା ଆପଣାର ମନକୁ ବଦଳାଇ ମିସରକୁ ଫେରିଯାଇ ପାରନ୍ତି।”	ମୋଶାଙ୍କ ଲିଖିତ ଦ୍ୱିତୀୟ ପୁସ୍ତକ ୧୩:୧୭	କାରଣ ମନୁଷ୍ୟପୁତ୍ର ମଧ୍ୟ ସେବା ପାଇବାକୁ ଆସି ନାହାଁନ୍ତି, ମାତ୍ର ସେବା କରିବାକୁ ଓ ଅନେକଙ୍କ ନିମନ୍ତେ ମୁକ୍ତିର ମୂଲ୍ୟ ସ୍ୱରୂପେ ଆପଣା ପ୍ରାଣ ଦେବାକୁ ଆସିଅଛନ୍ତି ।	ମାର୍କ ୧୦:୪୫	ପାଉଲ, ଖ୍ରୀଷ୍ଟ ଯୀଶୁଙ୍କ ଦାସ ଓ ଆହୂତ ଜଣେ ପ୍ରେରିତ, ପୁଣି, ଈଶ୍ୱର ଆପଣା ପୁତ୍ର ଆମ୍ଭମାନଙ୍କ ପ୍ରଭୁ ଯୀଶୁଖ୍ରୀଷ୍ଟଙ୍କ ସମ୍ବନ୍ଧରେ ନିଜର ଯେଉଁ ସୁସମାଚାର ଧର୍ମଶାସ୍ତ୍ରରେ ଆପଣା ଭାବବାଦୀମାନଙ୍କ ଦ୍ୱାରା ପୂର୍ବରେ ପ୍ରତିଜ୍ଞା କରିଥିଲେ,</Value><Br /><Value>ସେହି ସୁସମାଚାର ନିମନ୍ତେ ପୃଥକୀକୃତ,	ରୋମୀୟ ୧:୧	ଅତଏବ, ତୁମ୍ଭେମାନେ ଯାଇ ସମସ୍ତ ଜାତିର ଲୋକଙ୍କୁ ପିତା, ପୁତ୍ର ଓ ପବିତ୍ର ଆତ୍ମାଙ୍କ ନାମରେ ବାପ୍ତିସ୍ମ ଦେଇ,	ମାଥିଉ ୨୮:୧୯	END
